The Dispatcher interface defines the Dispatch method that processes webhook calls with admission attributes.\\n\\n## Configuration Management\\n\\nThe webhook configurations are managed by two configuration managers:\\n- mutatingWebhookConfigurationManager (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go) implements the generic.Source interface and watches MutatingWebhookConfiguration objects\\n- validatingWebhookConfigurationManager (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go) implements the generic.Source interface and watches ValidatingWebhookConfiguration objects\\n\\nBoth managers use Kubernetes informers to dynamically track webhook configurations and provide them via the Source interface's Webhooks() method.\\n\\n## WebhookAccessor Abstraction Layer\\n\\nThe WebhookAccessor interface (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go) provides a common abstraction for both mutating and validating webhooks. Concrete implementations are:\\n- mutatingWebhookAccessor: wraps v1.MutatingWebhook and created by NewMutatingWebhookAccessor()\\n- validatingWebhookAccessor: wraps v1.ValidatingWebhook and created by NewValidatingWebhookAccessor()\\n\\nThis abstraction allows the generic webhook processing logic to work uniformly with both webhook types.\\n\\n## Mutating Webhook Dispatcher with Reinvocation Logic\\n\\nThe mutatingDispatcher (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go) implements sequential webhook invocation with critical reinvocation logic. When Dispatch is called, it:\\n\\n1. Retrieves or creates a webhookReinvokeContext from the admission attributes' reinvocation context\\n2. Tracks the object state before webhook invocations\\n3. Iterates through webhooks sequentially, invoking each one\\n4. If the object is modified by a previous admission plugin, it determines which webhooks should be reinvoked\\n5. Stores patch information in audit annotations\\n\\nThe reinvocation mechanism uses webhookReinvokeContext (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/reinvocationcontext.go) to track:\\n- lastWebhookOutput: The object state after the last webhook invocation\\n- previouslyInvokedReinvocableWebhooks: Webhooks that have been invoked\\n- reinvokeWebhooks: Webhooks that should be reinvoked during the current reinvocation phase\\n\\nThis ensures that if in-tree admission plugins mutate the object, previously invoked webhooks that should react to those changes are called again.\\n\\n## Validating Webhook Dispatcher with Parallel Dispatch\\n\\nThe validatingDispatcher (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go) implements parallel webhook invocation for performance. When Dispatch is called, it:\\n\\n1. First determines all relevant webhooks by matching rules, namespace selectors, and object selectors sequentially\\n2. Pre-creates versioned attributes for all matched webhooks and caches them in a map\\n3. Spawns goroutines for each relevant webhook to invoke them in parallel\\n4. Uses sync.WaitGroup and error channels to coordinate parallel execution\\n5. Collects errors from all webhooks and returns early if any webhook denies the request\\n\\nThe versionedAttributeAccessor caches versioned attributes to allow efficient reuse across parallel webhook calls, avoiding redundant object conversions.\\n\\n## API Type Definitions\\n\\nThe MutatingWebhookConfiguration and ValidatingWebhookConfiguration types are defined in the kubernetes-api repository:\\n- admissionregistration/v1/types.go: Contains the current stable GA API versions\\n- admissionregistration/v1beta1/types.go: Contains deprecated v1beta1 API versions\\n\\nMutatingWebhookConfiguration contains a list of MutatingWebhook objects, each specifying rules, client configuration, failure policy, namespace/object selectors, and side effects. ValidatingWebhookConfiguration similarly contains ValidatingWebhook objects with the same matching and configuration fields.\\n\\n## Processing Flow\\n\\nWhen an admission request is made:\\n1. The plugin's Admit (for mutating) or Validate (for validating) method is called\\n2. This invokes the generic Webhook's Dispatch method\\n3. Dispatch calls the dispatcher's Dispatch method\\n4. The dispatcher retrieves webhooks from the configuration manager's Source\\n5. For mutating webhooks: sequential invocation with reinvocation tracking for object changes\\n6. For validating webhooks: parallel invocation with pre-cached versioned attributes\\n7. Results are collected and the request is either admitted, rejected, or admitted with modifications (mutating only)\\n\\nThe entire system is dynamic - webhook configurations are watched by informers and changes are reflected immediately without requiring API server restart.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1309,"cache_read_input_tokens":86264,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1309},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"7f830cd7-8d17-4e9e-ac68-d4bac640401c","uuid":"01b9145f-888f-4a12-9eeb-0a6b3e9ce07b"}
